; Function Attrs: nounwind willreturn
declare void @llvm.assume(i1) #1

; Function Attrs: noinline
define internal fastcc i32 @tvmgen_default_fused_layout_transform_compute_(i8* noalias align 64 %0, i8* noalias align 64 %1) unnamed_addr #2 {
entry:
  %2 = alloca %closure_loop_parallel_ax0.ax1.fused, align 8
  %3 = bitcast %closure_loop_parallel_ax0.ax1.fused* %2 to i8**
  store i8* %0, i8** %3, align 8
  %4 = getelementptr inbounds %closure_loop_parallel_ax0.ax1.fused, %closure_loop_parallel_ax0.ax1.fused* %2, i64 0, i32 1
  store i8* %1, i8** %4, align 8
  %5 = load i32 (i32 (i32, %0*, i8*)*, i8*, i32)*, i32 (i32 (i32, %0*, i8*)*, i8*, i32)** @__TVMBackendParallelLaunch, align 8, !tbaa !20
  %6 = bitcast %closure_loop_parallel_ax0.ax1.fused* %2 to i8*
  %7 = call i32 %5(i32 (i32, %0*, i8*)* nonnull @__tvm_parallel_lambda, i8* nonnull %6, i32 0)
  ret i32 %7
}

; Function Attrs: nofree norecurse nounwind
define private i32 @__tvm_parallel_lambda(i32 %task_id, %0* nocapture readonly %0, i8* nocapture readonly %1) #3 {
parallel_closure_entry:
  %2 = bitcast i8* %1 to half**
  %T_layout_trans1 = load half*, half** %2, align 8
  %3 = getelementptr inbounds i8, i8* %1, i64 8
  %4 = bitcast i8* %3 to half**
  %p02 = load half*, half** %4, align 8
  %5 = getelementptr inbounds %0, %0* %0, i64 0, i32 1
  %num_task = load i32, i32* %5, align 4
  %6 = add nsw i32 %num_task, 126591
  %7 = sdiv i32 %6, %num_task
  %8 = add nsw i32 %task_id, 1
  %9 = mul nsw i32 %7, %8
  %10 = icmp slt i32 %9, 126592
  %11 = select i1 %10, i32 %9, i32 126592
  %12 = mul nsw i32 %7, %task_id
  %13 = icmp slt i32 %12, 126592
  %14 = select i1 %13, i32 %12, i32 126592
  %15 = icmp slt i32 %14, %11
  br i1 %15, label %for_begin_ax2.outer.preheader.preheader, label %for_end_ax0.ax1.fused, !prof !19

for_begin_ax2.outer.preheader.preheader:          ; preds = %parallel_closure_entry
  %16 = sext i32 %14 to i64

; Function Attrs: noinline
define internal fastcc i32 @tvmgen_default_fused_nn_contrib_dense_pack_compute_(i8* noalias align 64 %0, i8* noalias align 64 %1, i8* noalias align 64 %2) unnamed_addr #2 {
entry:
  %3 = alloca %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused, align 8
  %4 = bitcast %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused* %3 to i8**
  store i8* %0, i8** %4, align 8
  %5 = getelementptr inbounds %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused, %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused* %3, i64 0, i32 1
  store i8* %1, i8** %5, align 8
  %6 = getelementptr inbounds %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused, %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused* %3, i64 0, i32 2
  store i8* %2, i8** %6, align 8
  %7 = load i32 (i32 (i32, %0*, i8*)*, i8*, i32)*, i32 (i32 (i32, %0*, i8*)*, i8*, i32)** @__TVMBackendParallelLaunch, align 8, !tbaa !20
  %8 = bitcast %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused* %3 to i8*
  %9 = call i32 %7(i32 (i32, %0*, i8*)* nonnull @__tvm_parallel_lambda.41, i8* nonnull %8, i32 0)
  ret i32 %9
}

; Function Attrs: nofree nounwind
define private i32 @__tvm_parallel_lambda.41(i32 %task_id, %0* nocapture readonly %0, i8* nocapture readonly %1) #4 {
parallel_closure_entry:
  %2 = bitcast i8* %1 to half**
  %p02 = load half*, half** %2, align 8
  %3 = getelementptr inbounds i8, i8* %1, i64 8
  %4 = bitcast i8* %3 to half**
  %p13 = load half*, half** %4, align 8
  %5 = getelementptr inbounds i8, i8* %1, i64 16
  %6 = bitcast i8* %5 to half**
  %compute4 = load half*, half** %6, align 8
  %7 = getelementptr inbounds %0, %0* %0, i64 0, i32 1
  %num_task = load i32, i32* %7, align 4
  %8 = add nsw i32 %num_task, 171
  %9 = sdiv i32 %8, %num_task
  %10 = add nsw i32 %task_id, 1
  %11 = mul nsw i32 %9, %10
  %12 = icmp slt i32 %11, 172
  %13 = select i1 %12, i32 %11, i32 172
  %14 = mul nsw i32 %9, %task_id
  %15 = icmp slt i32 %14, 172
  %16 = select i1 %15, i32 %14, i32 172
  %17 = icmp slt i32 %16, %13
  br i1 %17, label %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader.preheader, label %for_end_x.outer.y.outer.fused, !prof !19

for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader.preheader: ; preds = %parallel_closure_entry
  %scevgep98 = getelementptr half, half* %p02, i64 10304
  %scevgep120 = getelementptr half, half* %p13, i64 47104
  %scevgep125 = getelementptr half, half* %p02, i64 10304
  br label %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader

for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader: ; preds = %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader.preheader, %for_end_k.outer.1
  %x.outer.y.outer.fused23 = phi i32 [ %145, %for_end_k.outer.1 ], [ %16, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader.preheader ]
  %lsr150 = trunc i32 %x.outer.y.outer.fused23 to i2
  %18 = zext i2 %lsr150 to i64
  %19 = mul nuw nsw i64 %18, 11776
  %scevgep126 = getelementptr half, half* %scevgep125, i64 %19
  %20 = zext i2 %lsr150 to i64
  %21 = mul nuw nsw i64 %20, 11776
  %scevgep100 = getelementptr half, half* %scevgep98, i64 %21
  %22 = ashr i32 %x.outer.y.outer.fused23, 2
  %23 = shl i32 %22, 6
  %24 = and i32 %x.outer.y.outer.fused23, 3
  %25 = mul nuw nsw i32 %24, 22016
  %26 = add nsw i32 %25, %23
  %27 = mul nsw i32 %22, 94208
  %28 = sext i32 %26 to i64
  %29 = sext i32 %27 to i64
  %scevgep = getelementptr half, half* %p13, i64 %29
  br label %for_body_k.outer

for_end_x.outer.y.outer.fused:                    ; preds = %for_end_k.outer.1, %parallel_closure_entry
  ret i32 0

for_body_k.outer:                                 ; preds = %for_body_k.outer, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader
  %lsr.iv101 = phi i64 [ %math, %for_body_k.outer ], [ -1472, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader ]
  %lsr.iv = phi half* [ %scevgep96, %for_body_k.outer ], [ %scevgep, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader ]
  %compute.global1.sroa.0.020 = phi <32 x half> [ zeroinitializer, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader ], [ %34, %for_body_k.outer ]
  %compute.global1.sroa.4.019 = phi <32 x half> [ zeroinitializer, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader ], [ %38, %for_body_k.outer ]
  %compute.global1.sroa.8.018 = phi <32 x half> [ zeroinitializer, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader ], [ %42, %for_body_k.outer ]
  %compute.global1.sroa.12.017 = phi <32 x half> [ zeroinitializer, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader ], [ %46, %for_body_k.outer ]
  %compute.global1.sroa.16.016 = phi <32 x half> [ zeroinitializer, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader ], [ %50, %for_body_k.outer ]
  %compute.global1.sroa.20.015 = phi <32 x half> [ zeroinitializer, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader ], [ %54, %for_body_k.outer ]
  %compute.global1.sroa.24.014 = phi <32 x half> [ zeroinitializer, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader ], [ %58, %for_body_k.outer ]
  %compute.global1.sroa.28.013 = phi <32 x half> [ zeroinitializer, %for_begin_y.inner.outer.x.inner.outer.fused.preheader ], [ %62, %for_body_k.outer ]
  %lsr.iv97 = bitcast half* %lsr.iv to <32 x half>*
  %scevgep103 = getelementptr half, half* %scevgep100, i64 %lsr.iv101
  %scevgep104 = getelementptr half, half* %scevgep103, i64 -8832
  %30 = load half, half* %scevgep104, align 2, !tbaa !198
  %31 = insertelement <32 x half> undef, half %30, i32 0
  %32 = shufflevector <32 x half> %31, <32 x half> undef, <32 x i32> zeroinitializer

; Function Attrs: noinline
define internal fastcc i32 @tvmgen_default_fused_nn_contrib_dense_pack_1_compute_(i8* noalias align 64 %0, i8* noalias align 64 %1, i8* noalias align 64 %2) unnamed_addr #2 {
entry:
  %3 = alloca %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused.0, align 8
  %4 = bitcast %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused.0* %3 to i8**
  store i8* %0, i8** %4, align 8
  %5 = getelementptr inbounds %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused.0, %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused.0* %3, i64 0, i32 1
  store i8* %1, i8** %5, align 8
  %6 = getelementptr inbounds %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused.0, %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused.0* %3, i64 0, i32 2
  store i8* %2, i8** %6, align 8
  %7 = load i32 (i32 (i32, %0*, i8*)*, i8*, i32)*, i32 (i32 (i32, %0*, i8*)*, i8*, i32)** @__TVMBackendParallelLaunch, align 8, !tbaa !20
  %8 = bitcast %closure_loop_parallel_x.outer.y.outer.fused.0* %3 to i8*
  %9 = call i32 %7(i32 (i32, %0*, i8*)* nonnull @__tvm_parallel_lambda.50, i8* nonnull %8, i32 0)
  ret i32 %9

define dllexport i32 @tvmgen_default_fused_nn_sparse_dense(i8* noalias nocapture readonly %args, i32* noalias nocapture readonly %arg_type_ids, i32 %num_args, i8* noalias nocapture readnone %out_ret_value, i32* noalias nocapture readnone %out_ret_tcode, i8* noalias nocapture readnone %resource_handle) local_unnamed_addr #0 !dbg !313 {
entry:
  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata i8* %args, metadata !315, metadata !DIExpression()), !dbg !321
  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata i32* %arg_type_ids, metadata !316, metadata !DIExpression()), !dbg !321
  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata i32 %num_args, metadata !317, metadata !DIExpression()), !dbg !321
  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata i8* %out_ret_value, metadata !318, metadata !DIExpression()), !dbg !321
  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata i32* %out_ret_tcode, metadata !319, metadata !DIExpression()), !dbg !321
  call void @llvm.dbg.value(metadata i8* %resource_handle, metadata !320, metadata !DIExpression()), !dbg !321
  %0 = icmp eq i32 %num_args, 5, !dbg !321

; Function Attrs: nofree noinline nounwind
define internal fastcc void @tvmgen_default_fused_nn_sparse_dense_compute_(i8* noalias nocapture align 64 %0, i8* noalias nocapture readonly align 64 %1, i8* noalias nocapture readonly align 64 %2, i8* noalias nocapture readonly align 64 %3, i8* noalias nocapture readonly align 64 %4) unnamed_addr #6 {
entry:
  %5 = bitcast i8* %1 to i32*
  %.pre.pre = load i32, i32* %5, align 64, !tbaa !452
  %scevgep = getelementptr i8, i8* %4, i64 12
  %scevgep23 = getelementptr i8, i8* %2, i64 6
  br label %for_begin_row.preheader

for_begin_row.preheader:                          ; preds = %for_end_row, %entry
  %indvar = phi i64 [ 0, %entry ], [ %indvar.next, %for_end_row ]
  %6 = mul nuw nsw i64 %indvar, 2752
  %7 = trunc i64 %6 to i32
  br label %for_body_row

for_end_i:                                        ; preds = %for_end_row
  ret void

for_begin_elem_idx.for_begin_row.loopexit_crit_edge.unr-lcssa: ; preds = %for_body_elem_idx, %for_body_elem_idx.lr.ph
  %.lcssa.ph = phi half [ undef, %for_body_elem_idx.lr.ph ], [ %75, %for_body_elem_idx ]
  %indvars.iv.unr = phi i64 [ 0, %for_body_elem_idx.lr.ph ], [ %indvars.iv.next.3, %for_body_elem_idx ]
  %.unr = phi half [ 0xH0000, %for_body_elem_idx.lr.ph ], [ %75, %for_body_elem_idx ]
  %lcmp.mod = icmp eq i64 %xtraiter, 0
  br i1 %lcmp.mod, label %for_begin_elem_idx.for_begin_row.loopexit_crit_edge, label %for_body_elem_idx.epil.preheader

for_body_elem_idx.epil.preheader:                 ; preds = %for_begin_elem_idx.for_begin_row.loopexit_crit_edge.unr-lcssa
  %8 = add nsw i64 %indvars.iv.unr, %32
  %9 = shl i64 %8, 2
  %scevgep36 = getelementptr i8, i8* %4, i64 %9
  %10 = shl i64 %8, 1
  %scevgep39 = getelementptr i8, i8* %2, i64 %10
  br label %for_body_elem_idx.epil

for_body_elem_idx.epil:                           ; preds = %for_body_elem_idx.epil.preheader, %for_body_elem_idx.epil
  %lsr.iv = phi i64 [ 0, %for_body_elem_idx.epil.preheader ], [ %lsr.iv.next, %for_body_elem_idx.epil ]
  %11 = phi half [ %21, %for_body_elem_idx.epil ], [ %.unr, %for_body_elem_idx.epil.preheader ]
  %12 = bitcast i8* %3 to half*
  %13 = shl nuw nsw i64 %lsr.iv, 1
  %scevgep40 = getelementptr i8, i8* %scevgep39, i64 %13
  %scevgep4041 = bitcast i8* %scevgep40 to half*
  %14 = load half, half* %scevgep4041, align 2, !tbaa !454
  %15 = shl nuw nsw i64 %lsr.iv, 2
  %scevgep37 = getelementptr i8, i8* %scevgep36, i64 %15
  %scevgep3738 = bitcast i8* %scevgep37 to i32*
  %16 = load i32, i32* %scevgep3738, align 4, !tbaa !456
  %17 = sext i32 %16 to i64
  %promoted = sext i32 %7 to i64
  %18 = add nsw i64 %17, %promoted
  %19 = getelementptr inbounds half, half* %12, i64 %18
  %20 = load half, half* %19, align 2, !tbaa !458
  %21 = tail call half @llvm.fmuladd.f16(half %14, half %20, half %11)
  %lsr.iv.next = add nuw nsw i64 %lsr.iv, 1
  %epil.iter.cmp = icmp eq i64 %xtraiter, %lsr.iv.next
  br i1 %epil.iter.cmp, label %for_begin_elem_idx.for_begin_row.loopexit_crit_edge, label %for_body_elem_idx.epil, !llvm.loop !460

for_begin_elem_idx.for_begin_row.loopexit_crit_edge: ; preds = %for_body_elem_idx.epil, %for_begin_elem_idx.for_begin_row.loopexit_crit_edge.unr-lcssa
  %.lcssa = phi half [ %.lcssa.ph, %for_begin_elem_idx.for_begin_row.loopexit_crit_edge.unr-lcssa ], [ %21, %for_body_elem_idx.epil ]
  %sunkaddr = mul i64 %26, 2
  %sunkaddr42 = getelementptr inbounds i8, i8* %0, i64 %sunkaddr
  %22 = bitcast i8* %sunkaddr42 to half*
  store half %.lcssa, half* %22, align 2, !tbaa !462
  br label %for_begin_row.loopexit

for_begin_row.loopexit:                           ; preds = %for_begin_elem_idx.for_begin_row.loopexit_crit_edge, %for_body_row
  %exitcond6 = icmp eq i64 %indvars.iv.next5, 2752
  br i1 %exitcond6, label %for_end_row, label %for_body_row, !prof !48

for_body_row:                                     ; preds = %for_begin_row.loopexit, %for_begin_row.preheader
  %23 = phi i32 [ %.pre.pre, %for_begin_row.preheader ], [ %29, %for_begin_row.loopexit ]
  %indvars.iv4 = phi i64 [ 0, %for_begin_row.preheader ], [ %indvars.iv.next5, %for_begin_row.loopexit ]
  %24 = bitcast i8* %1 to i32*
  %25 = bitcast i8* %0 to half*
  %26 = add nuw nsw i64 %indvars.iv4, %6
  %27 = getelementptr inbounds half, half* %25, i64 %26
  store half 0xH0000, half* %27, align 2, !tbaa !462
  %indvars.iv.next5 = add nuw nsw i64 %indvars.iv4, 1
  %28 = getelementptr inbounds i32, i32* %24, i64 %indvars.iv.next5
  %29 = load i32, i32* %28, align 4, !tbaa !452
  %30 = sub i32 %29, %23
  %31 = icmp sgt i32 %30, 0
